<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">圆锥曲线</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="noteTA" id="noteTA-6b75fab2"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group="Math" data-noteta-group-source="module"></div></div><div class="noteTA-local"><div data-noteta-code="zh-cn:实轴; zh-tw:贯轴"></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Secciones_Conicas.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" decoding="async" height="175" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Secciones_Conicas.svg/280px-Secciones_Conicas.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Secciones_Conicas.svg/420px-Secciones_Conicas.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/Secciones_Conicas.svg/560px-Secciones_Conicas.svg.png 2x" width="280"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Secciones_Conicas.svg" title="放大"></a></div>圆锥曲线</div></div></div>
<p><b>圆锥曲线</b>（<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E8%AA%9E" title="英语">英语</a>：conic section），又称<b>圆锥截痕</b>、<b>圆锥截面</b>、<b>二次平面曲线</b>，是<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%AD%B8" title="几何学">几何学</a>中透过平切<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5" title="圆锥">圆锥</a>（严格为一个正圆锥面和一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="平面 (数学)">平面</a>完整相切）得到的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="曲线">曲线</a>，包括<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%AD%E5%9C%86" title="椭圆">椭圆</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%9B%E7%89%A9%E7%BA%BF" title="抛物线">抛物线</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8C%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="双曲线">双曲线</a>及一些退化类型。
</p><p>圆锥曲线在约西元前200年时就已被命名与研究，其发现者为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希腊">古希腊</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="数学家">数学家</a><a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E6%B3%A2%E7%BD%97%E5%B0%BC%E5%A5%A5%E6%96%AF" title="阿波罗尼奥斯">阿波罗尼奥斯</a>，当时阿波罗尼阿斯已对它们的性质做过系统性的研究。
</p><p>圆锥曲线应用最广泛的<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89" title="定义">定义</a>为（椭圆，抛物线，双曲线的统一定义）：动点到一定点（<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A6%E9%BB%9E_(%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95)" title="焦点 (几何)">焦点</a>）的距离与其到一定直线（<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%86%E7%BA%BF" title="准线">准线</a>）的距离之比为常数（<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%A2%E5%BF%83%E7%8E%87" title="离心率">离心率</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd253103f0876afc68ebead27a5aa9867d927467" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>）的点的集合是圆锥曲线。对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0&lt;e&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="0&lt;e&lt;1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/679de8c4138507493a1cc5adc572bb0ffdd19a82" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:9.605ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>得到椭圆，对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>

</math></span><img alt="e&gt;1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9605ca17e3915b659685c0326fbbcbfb522f11b3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.344ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>得到双曲线。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle F}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>F</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle F}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="F" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/545fd099af8541605f7ee55f08225526be88ce57" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.741ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E9%BB%9E" title="定点">定点</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle l}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>l</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle l}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="l" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/829091f745070b9eb97a80244129025440a1cfac" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.693ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>为定<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF" title="直线">直线</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd253103f0876afc68ebead27a5aa9867d927467" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为正<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B0" title="常数">常数</a>，称满足<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {|PF|}{|Pl|}}=e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mrow>

<mo>=</mo>
<mi>e</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {|PF|}{|Pl|}}=e}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {|PF|}{|Pl|}}=e}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c2cb224ce4429c30dc797d39a50f0a8ab98caf13" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:9.798ex; height:6.509ex;"/></span>的动点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle P}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="P" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4dc73bf40314945ff376bd363916a738548d40a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.745ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的轨迹为<b>圆锥曲线</b>。
</p><p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle F}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="F" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/545fd099af8541605f7ee55f08225526be88ce57" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.741ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>为其<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A6%E9%BB%9E" title="焦点">焦点</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle l}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>l</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle l}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="l" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/829091f745070b9eb97a80244129025440a1cfac" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.693ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%86%E7%BA%BF" title="准线">准线</a>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd253103f0876afc68ebead27a5aa9867d927467" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.083ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A6%BB%E5%BF%83%E7%8E%87" title="离心率">离心率</a>。
</p><p>由此可知，圆锥曲线的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87" title="极坐标">极坐标</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%83%E6%95%B8%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="参数方程">参数方程</a>为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \rho =e(d-\rho \cos \theta )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \theta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>将参数方程转换成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%92%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87" title="直角坐标">直角坐标</a>方程易得，
</p>
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e=1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e=1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9c2f5932668126c63c844dc00ca187bc58a29e5a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.344ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>时，曲线为<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%9B%E7%89%A9%E7%BA%BF" title="抛物线">抛物线</a>。</dd>
<dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e\neq 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e\neq 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle e\neq 1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/52247da9ee900379e2c04733fba2ccb24f31d16a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.344ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>时，
<dl><dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0&lt;e&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<dd>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Conic_sections_with_plane.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="350" data-file-width="600" decoding="async" height="233" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Conic_sections_with_plane.svg/400px-Conic_sections_with_plane.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Conic_sections_with_plane.svg/600px-Conic_sections_with_plane.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Conic_sections_with_plane.svg/800px-Conic_sections_with_plane.svg.png 2x" width="400"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Conic_sections_with_plane.svg" title="放大"></a></div>圆锥曲线的类型：1.抛物线2.圆和椭圆3.双曲线</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%AD%E5%9C%86" title="椭圆">椭圆</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>：当平面只与圆锥面一侧相交，交截线是<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%97%AD%E5%90%88%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="闭合曲线（页面不存在）">闭合曲线</a>的时候，且不过圆锥顶点，结果为近似椭圆。如果截面与圆锥面的对称轴垂直，结果为圆。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%9B%E7%89%A9%E7%BA%BF" title="抛物线">抛物线</a>：截面仅与圆锥面的一条母线平行，结果为抛物线。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8C%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="双曲线">双曲线</a>：截面与圆锥面两侧都相交，且不过圆锥顶点，结果为双曲线。
</p><p>在平面通过圆锥的顶点的时候，有一些退化情况。交截线可以是一个直线、一个点、或一对直线。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.87.A0.E4.BD.95.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="几何性质">几何性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：几何性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E6.A4.AD.E5.9C.86.EF.BC.88ellipse.EF.BC.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="椭圆（ellipse）">椭圆（ellipse）</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：椭圆（ellipse）">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>椭圆上的点到两个焦点的距离和等于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%95%BF%E8%BD%B4" title="长轴">长轴</a>长（2a）。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.8A.9B.E7.89.A9.E7.BA.BF.EF.BC.88Parabola.EF.BC.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="抛物线（Parabola）">抛物线（Parabola）</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：抛物线（Parabola）">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>抛物线上的点到焦点的距离等于该点到<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%86%E7%BA%BF" title="准线">准线</a>的距离。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.8C.E6.9B.B2.E7.BA.BF.EF.BC.88Hyperbola.EF.BC.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="双曲线（Hyperbola）">双曲线（Hyperbola）</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：双曲线（Hyperbola）">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>双曲线上的点到两个焦点的距离之差的绝对值等于贯轴长（2a）。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.A6.BB.E5.BF.83.E7.8E.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="离心率">离心率</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：离心率">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eccentricity.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="463" data-file-width="455" decoding="async" height="285" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Eccentricity.svg/280px-Eccentricity.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Eccentricity.svg/420px-Eccentricity.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Eccentricity.svg/560px-Eccentricity.svg.png 2x" width="280"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eccentricity.svg" title="放大"></a></div>有固定焦点<i>F</i>和准线的<font color="ff0000">圆（<i>e</i>=0) </font>、<font color="#ff8a00">椭圆（<i>e</i>=1/2）</font>、<font color="#00ff00">抛物线 (<i>e</i>=1)</font>和<font color="#0000ff">双曲线（<i>e</i>=2）</font>。</div></div></div>
<p>对于椭圆和双曲线，可以采用两种焦点-准线组合，每个都给出同样完整的椭圆或双曲线。从中心到准线的距离是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a/e\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo>/</mo>
</mrow>
<mi>e</mi>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a/e\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a/e \ " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5751ce8183d264b423d034721faeab6b291db274" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.056ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，这里的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a \ " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cab11b679bd92051611e727cc8cc095c5c883745" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.81ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>是椭圆的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E9%95%BF%E8%BD%B4" title="半长轴">半长轴</a>，或双曲线的半实轴。从中心到焦点的距离是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle ae\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mi>e</mi>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle ae\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="ae \ " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/682ad77a5d79000421a436a6731655045ecd663e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.894ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>在圆的情况下，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d9850169d70a5ab7df71c2126441a86cec93eec8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.344ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>且准线被假想为离中心无限远。这时声称圆由距离是到L的距离的e倍的所有点组成是没有意义的。
</p><p>圆锥曲线的离心率因此是对它偏离于圆的程度的度量。
</p><p>对于一个给定的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a \ " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cab11b679bd92051611e727cc8cc095c5c883745" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.81ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>e</mi>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle e\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e \ " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a4204fc2368e201092faf08ddfcb3d4781dd7b53" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.664ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>越接近于1，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E7%9F%AD%E8%BD%B4" title="半短轴">半短轴</a>就越小。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.AC.9B.E5.8D.A1.E5.B0.94.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="笛卡尔坐标">笛卡尔坐标</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：笛卡尔坐标">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E7%AC%9B%E5%8D%A1%E5%B0%94%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87%E7%B3%BB" title="笛卡尔坐标系">笛卡尔坐标系</a>内，二元<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="二次方程">二次方程</a>的图像可以表示圆锥曲线，并且所有圆锥曲线都以这种方式引出。方程有如下形式
</p>

<mo>=</mo>

</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left[{\begin{matrix}x&amp;y&amp;1\end{matrix}}\right]\left[{\begin{matrix}A&amp;B/2&amp;D/2\\B/2&amp;C&amp;E/2\\D/2&amp;E/2&amp;F\end{matrix}}\right]\left[{\begin{matrix}x\\y\\1\end{matrix}}\right]=0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left[{\begin{matrix}x&amp;y&amp;1\end{matrix}}\right]\left[{\begin{matrix}A&amp;B/2&amp;D/2\\B/2&amp;C&amp;E/2\\D/2&amp;E/2&amp;F\end{matrix}}\right]\left[{\begin{matrix}x\\y\\1\end{matrix}}\right]=0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a69f6b1ee2f4d7f828fb8c7e89c4e60536c2a14e" style="vertical-align: -4.338ex; width:41.651ex; height:9.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这是在射影几何中使用的齐次形式的一个特例。 (参见<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF#齐次坐标" title="圆锥曲线">齐次坐标</a>)

<h3><span id=".E9.A1.9E.E5.88.A5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="类别">类别</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：类别">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>借由<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{Q}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A_{Q}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A_{Q}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/efc37732dbc2418bc356a1c39b525844b8546972" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:3.275ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，我们可以判定圆锥曲线是否退化。
</p>
<ul><li>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \det(A_{Q})=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \det(A_{Q})\neq 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>若圆锥曲线未发生退化，则<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Protter_1970_326_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-Protter_1970_326-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>若 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \det(A_{33})&gt;0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<li>若 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \det(A_{33})=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.8D.E8.AE.8A.E9.87.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="不变量">不变量</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：不变量">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>矩阵<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{Q}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

<h3><span id=".E8.BD.89.E6.8F.9B.E7.88.B2.E6.A8.99.E6.BA.96.E6.96.B9.E7.A8.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="转换爲标准方程">转换爲标准方程</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：转换爲标准方程">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>对于椭圆或双曲线，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Q}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mi>Q</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<h2><span id=".E6.9E.81.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="极坐标">极坐标</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：极坐标">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Elps-slr.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="285" data-file-width="512" decoding="async" height="167" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Elps-slr.svg/300px-Elps-slr.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Elps-slr.svg/450px-Elps-slr.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/35/Elps-slr.svg/600px-Elps-slr.svg.png 2x" width="300"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Elps-slr.svg" title="放大"></a></div>椭圆的半正焦弦</div></div></div>
<p>圆锥曲线的<b>半正焦弦</b>（semi-latus rectum）通常指示为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \ell }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \ell }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\ell " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f066e981e530bacc07efc6a10fa82deee985929e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.97ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，是从单一焦点或两个焦点中的一个，到圆锥曲线自身的，沿着垂直于主轴（长轴）的直线度量的距离。它有关于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E9%95%BF%E8%BD%B4" title="半长轴">半长轴</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8D%8A%E7%9F%AD%E8%BD%B4" title="半短轴">半短轴</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>b</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle b}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，通过公式<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\ell =b^{2}\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>b</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a\ell =b^{2}\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle a\ell =b^{2}\ }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/903c7ebea812f17872e9d327d932051e154a352f" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.93ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>或<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \ell =a(1-e^{2})\ }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<msup>
<mi>e</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mtext> </mtext>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \ell =a(1-e^{2})\ }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \ell =a(1-e^{2})\ }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3174774bdff736fbb8df1da286eb439e17417fa6" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:13.828ex; height:3.176ex;"/></span>。
</p><p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87" title="极坐标">极坐标系</a>中，圆锥曲线有一个焦点在原点，如果有另一个焦点的话它在正<i>x</i>轴上，给出自方程
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle r={\ell  \over (1-e\cos \theta )}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>r</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>
<mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>e</mi>
<mi>cos</mi>
<mo>⁡<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
<mi>θ<!-- θ --></mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle r={\ell  \over (1-e\cos \theta )}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle r={\ell  \over (1-e\cos \theta )}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b0eb040fa2eda870ae20fd17d78e0e8acaff70c8" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:16.855ex; height:6.176ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>或者，
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{r}}={\frac {1}{\ell }}(1-e\cos \theta )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{r}}={\frac {1}{\ell }}(1-e\cos \theta )}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{r}}={\frac {1}{\ell }}(1-e\cos \theta )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/773c0e901849c86f537a3605110dd11cb99a830c" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:18.967ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>，</dd></dl>
<p>如上，对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle e=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="e=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d9850169d70a5ab7df71c2126441a86cec93eec8" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.344ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>得到一个圆，对于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0&lt;e&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h2><span id=".E9.BD.90.E6.AC.A1.E5.9D.90.E6.A0.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="齐次坐标">齐次坐标</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：齐次坐标">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在<a href="/wiki/%E9%BD%90%E6%AC%A1%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87" title="齐次坐标">齐次坐标</a>下圆锥曲线可以表示为：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}x^{2}+A_{2}y^{2}+A_{3}z^{2}+2B_{1}xy+2B_{2}xz+2B_{3}yz=0\;}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta &gt;0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\delta &gt;0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/595d5cea06fdcaf2642caf549eda2cfc537958a9" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.31ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}=A_{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A_{1}=A_{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A_{1}=A_{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4ccb4687bbe819cd8e1f6c6afb06b9316a6c18b2" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:8.693ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，圆锥曲线是<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>；如果<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \delta &lt;0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>δ<!-- δ --></mi>
<mo>&lt;</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta &lt;0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \delta &lt;0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/18c6e67daff412fd88869d292c618a1140ff42da" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.31ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A_{1}=-A_{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>A</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A_{1}=-A_{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A_{1}=-A_{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/00e17ca3d1c27dd62c893db8d353a0aa9a7c826c" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.501ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，它是直角<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8C%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="双曲线">双曲线</a>。可以证明在<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E5%B0%84%E5%BD%B1%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="复射影平面">复射影平面</a><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {CP} ^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">C</mi>
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">P</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {CP} ^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathbb{CP}^2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8315f9899686d13d0a0bd74c069122bec47ddad9" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:4.153ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>中，两个圆锥曲线共有四个点（如果考虑<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%87%8D%E6%A0%B9" title="重根">重根</a>），所以永不多于4个交点并总有1个交点（可能性：4个不同的交点，2个单一交点和1个双重交点，2个双重交点，1单一交点和1个三重交点，1个四重交点）。如果存在至少一个重根<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle &gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>&gt;</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle &gt;1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle &gt;1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/95b523fe1c29f36fef6670b3c78f20087c5dceed" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.616ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的交点，则两个圆锥曲线被称为<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%87%E7%BA%BF" title="切线">相切</a>的。如果只有一个四重交点，两个圆锥曲线被称为是<a href="/wiki/%E6%8C%AF%E5%8A%A8" title="振动">共振</a>的。
</p><p>进一步的，每个<a href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E7%BA%BF" title="直线">直线</a>与每个圆锥曲线相交两次。如果两交点是重合成一点，则这个线被称为<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%87%E7%BA%BF" title="切线">切线</a>。因为所有直线交圆锥曲线两次，每个圆锥曲线有两个点在<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E5%B0%84%E5%BD%B1%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2" title="实射影平面">无穷远</a>（与<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E7%AA%AE%E9%81%A0%E7%B7%9A" title="无穷远线">无穷远线</a>的交点）。如果这些点是实数的，圆锥曲线必定是<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8C%E6%9B%B2%E7%BA%BF" title="双曲线">双曲线</a>；如果它们是虚共轭，圆锥曲线必定是<a href="/wiki/%E6%A4%AD%E5%9C%86" title="椭圆">椭圆</a>，如果圆锥曲线有双重点在无穷远，则它是<a href="/wiki/%E6%8A%9B%E7%89%A9%E7%BA%BF" title="抛物线">抛物线</a>。如果在无穷远的点是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (1,i,0)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>i</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (1,i,0)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (1,i,0)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0c0e716e7c07e3e8ae0250765594442e6ed60f45" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:7.005ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (1,-i,0)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>i</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (1,-i,0)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (1,-i,0)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a0756172a1c2f1ddfcd53f306da37c44243c8a1f" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.813ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>，则圆锥曲线是<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86" title="圆">圆</a>。如果圆锥曲线有一个实数点和一个虚数点在无穷远，或它有两个不共轭的虚数点，它不是抛物线、不是椭圆、不是双曲线。
</p>
